ImPORTANT  NOTICE  REGARDING  ACCEPTANCE  Of  NOTICES 
fOR  PubLICATION  IN  ThE  WEEkLy  “GAzETTE”
AttENtiON is drawn to the Notification appearing in the 1st week of every month, regarding the latest dates and times of acceptance of Notices 
for publication in the weekly Gazettes, at the end of every weekly Gazette of Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka.
All notices to be published in the weekly Gazettes shall close at 12.00 noon of each friday, two weeks before the date of publication. 
All Government Departments, Corporations, Boards, etc. are hereby advised that Notifications fixing closing dates and times of applications in 
respect of Post-Vacancies, Examinations, tender Notices and dates and times of Auction Sales, etc. should be prepared by giving adequate time 
both from the date of despatch of notices to Govt. Press and from the date of publication, thereby enabling those interested in the contents of such 
notices to actively and positively participate please note that inquiries and complaints made in respect of corrections pertaining to notification 
will not be entertained after three months from the date of publication.
All Notices to be published in the weekly Gazette should reach Government Press two weeks before the date of publication i.e. Notices 
for publication in the weekly Gazette of 02nd November, 2017 should reach Government Press on or before 12.00 noon on 20th October, 2017.
Electronic Transactions Act, No. 19 of  2006 - Section 9
“Where any Act or enactment provides that any proclamation, rule, regulation, order, by-law, notification or other matter shall be 
published in the Gazette, then such requirement shall be deemed to have been satisfied if such rule, regulation, order, by-law, notification or 
other matter is published in an electronic form of the Gazette.”
 
GanGani LiyanaGe,
 Government Printer (Acting).
Department of Govt. Printing, 
Colombo 08,
01st January, 2017.
  This Gazette can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
1557 - B 81215 - 403 (2017/10)
Note.–  (i) Local Authorities (Special Provisions) Bill was published as a supplement to the Part ii  of the Gazette of the Democratic 
Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka of September 29, 2017. 
 (ii) Anti-Dumping and Countervailing Duties Bill was published as a supplement to the Part ii of the Gazette of the Democratic 
Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka of October 06, 2017. 
 (iii) Safeguard Measures Bill was published as a supplement to the Part ii of the Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic 
of Sri Lanka of October 06, 2017.

PART  I :  SEC.  (I) – GAZETTE OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA – 13.10.2017
1615
Government Notifications 
INSTRuCTIONS  TO  ISSuE mEDIA 
ACCREDITATION CARDS by ThE 
DEPARTmENT Of
GOvERNmENT INfORmATION
DEPARtMENt of Government information issues media 
accreditation cards to journalists practicing in Sri Lanka 
with the purpose of facilitating their duties and protecting 
their professional rights and this will be issued with the 
sole recommendation of the head of the particular media 
station. thus, the all media heads are kindly requested to 
provide recommendation only for those who are deemed 
necessary for accreditation.
 02. Additional details on issuing of media accreditation 
cards which are not included in this document are 
stated in a separate attachment (1) for your kind 
perusal.
 03. Media accreditation cards will be issued as per 
following sectors, but not necessarily as per such 
category.
 i. Local Journalists 
  Journalists attached to a recognized local media 
institution on permanent or on contractual basis 
or journalists. Provincial journalists will not be 
identified as per their geographical presence 
and all journalists will be issued with a common 
“Journalist’’ accreditation. However, whether they 
are fulltime or part time factor will be identified. 
(P or f).
 ii. Photo Journalists
  Photo Journalists, who are serving at a recognized 
media institution on permanent or on contractual 
basis, for more than six months.
 iii. Web Journalists
  Website should be daily updated, should publish 
at least 25% of its content on news and current 
affairs, should have continuously maintained 
for six months and should be registered with 
the Ministry of finance and Media. Only two 
accreditation cards will be issued at the initial 
registration for each language web site.
  in case several websites are registered under one 
person or a company , only one website will be 
eligible to receive accreditation cards.
 iv. freelance Journalists
  Journalists who have continuously , within the 
past six months from the day of the application, 
presented more than 12 programmes /articles  
for a recognized print, broadcast or web media 
(published news items should be provided) will 
be eligible to apply.
 v. media Administrators
  Media administrators who are directly engaged 
in administrative responsibilities at a recognized 
media institution.
  Media institutions with 100 – 200 employees – 2 
identity cards
  Media institutions with 200 – 300 employees – 4 
identity cards
  Media institutions with more than 300 employees 
– 5 identity cards
 vi. Technical Staff (media Related)
  t echnical staff at a recognized media institution 
who regularly leave the office for duties related to 
news and / or current affairs coverage (especially 
for broadcast media).
 vii. foreign Journalists
  Permanent – Resident Journalists of foreign  
 media organizations or appointed 
   / accredited to Sri Lanka by a
    foreign media institution
  Temporary – Journalists who are on short
    assignments (less than three
    months)
 viii.  Media Officials
  Officials who are conducting media / information 
related duties at Government Departments and 
Ministries.
 ix. Tv Journalist  
  tV camera persons in a recognized media 
organization.
 x. Presenter
  Presenters at broadcast stations as recommended 
by station heads.
 xi. Tele Artist
  t ele drama makers, actors and production 
team members as recommended by respective 
associations. 
 04. Applications for accreditation are available at DGi  
or the online versions on DGi and news.lk websites. 
Applications for accreditation should include certified 
photocopy of the company iD, or a copy of the 
appointment letter.

<!-- page 60 -->

I fldgi : (I) fPoh    ‑ YS% ,xld m%cd;dka;s%l iudcjd§ ckrcfha .eiÜ m;%h ‑ 2017'10'13
PART  I :  SEC.  (I) – GAZETTE OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA – 13.10.2017
1616
 05. Duly filled applications should be forwarded to 
the Director General of Government information 
(electronically or manually) with 1 '' x 1 1/2 size, 
colour photographs and other relevant documents 
mentioned in the instructions. Media accreditation 
cards for local and Sri Lanka based media persons 
will be issued within within the first six months of 
each year and on special requirements until 30
th 
September. However, the final decision on issuing 
media accreditation will be made by the Director 
General of Government information.
 06. Media accreditation for Colombo based will be 
subjected to annual renewal while for others will be 
subjected to renewal once in two years. the head 
of the media institution should send a list of names 
who require accreditation for the prior approval of 
the Director General of Government information.
 Dr. 
ranga kalansOOriya,
 Director General of Government information. 
Attachment 01
general cOnditiOns
01. A maximum of 03 accreditation cards will be 
issued for monthly publications.
02. A maximum of 02 accreditation cards will be 
issued for publications printed once in two 
months.
 However, media institutions related to above 01 
and 02, should provide recently published 12 
subsequent copies in order to prove the continuity 
of its publication.
03. A supplement issued with a certain newspaper 
should not be considered as a separate newspaper 
and accreditation cards for journalists who have 
applied for accreditation in such supplements 
should be issued under the name of the main 
newspaper.
04. Head of the media institution is responsible of 
obtaining the accreditation card and forwarding  it 
to this department from a journalist who resigned/
dismissed from his media institution. Otherwise, 
a substitute accreditation card will not be issued.
05. t o obtain an accreditation card for a misplaced 
one, a request should be made by the relevant 
media institution along with a report of a police 
complaint.
06. Media accreditation will not be issued to 
publication and broadcast stations if they are not 
handling news and current affairs.
 Dr. 
ranga kalansOOriya,
 Director General of Government information.
